function calculateLifespan() {
  const mattressType = document.getElementById("mattress-type").value;
  const purchaseDate = document.getElementById("purchase-date").value;
  const usageFrequency = document.getElementById("usage-frequency").value;
  let lifespan;

  // Logic to determine lifespan based on mattress type and usage
  switch (mattressType) {
    case "innerspring":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 5 : 7;
      break;
    case "memory-foam":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 8 : 10;
      break;
    case "latex":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 12 : 15;
      break;
    case "hybrid":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 6 : 8;
      break;
    case "airbed":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 8 : 10;
      break;
    case "futon":
      lifespan = usageFrequency === "daily" ? 5 : 7;
      break;
    default:
      console.error("Invalid mattress type");
  }

  // Calculate the replacement date
  const purchaseDateObject = new Date(purchaseDate);
  const replacementDate = new Date(purchaseDateObject.getFullYear() + lifespan, purchaseDateObject.getMonth(), purchaseDateObject.getDate());

  // Display the result
  document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = `Based on your input, you should consider replacing your mattress by ${replacementDate.toLocaleDateString()}.`;
}		</style>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4221_e12faf-3d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4221_e12faf-3d">Featured Product of the Week</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4221_075f09-6c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4221_075f09-6c">The<strong> Philips Handheld Steamer 3000 Series, model STH3010/76</strong>, is a game-changer in the world of garment care.</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4221_683429-4c alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle">

<p class="kt-adv-heading_64d71e-4b wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading_64d71e-4b"><meta charset="utf-8"></meta>When you&#8217;re in a hurry, waiting for your garment care equipment to heat up can be frustrating.</p>
